Fourth Bank Issues Reserve Report

No. 152

The Fourth Bank Reserve is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jin Cheng, Zhongnan, and Continental Banks to handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the articles of association of the reserve, the issuance of banknotes is fully backed by reserves. Cash reserves must be at least 60%, and security reserves must be at most 40%. It is announced once a week after being audited by the auditors and accountants of the Fourth Bank. The 1153rd announcement of the Shanghai Reserve on December 3, 20, is recorded as follows:

Amount of banknotes in circulation: 25,331,157 yuan.

Total reserve amount: 25,331,157 yuan, including cash reserve of 17,514,757 yuan and security reserve of 7,816,400 yuan.

Reader's Advisor

(1) Discussion Regarding Ms. Zhang Yunqiu's Question

丨See December 3rd of this column

Mr. Shu Xiwu's message: (1) Due to men's inferior nature of liking the new and disliking the old, and women's inability to be independent, (2) women must strive for independence, otherwise they must endure considerably.

Mr. Cheng Jingjin's message: (1) For example, today the cook roasts a chicken. The first time we eat it, we feel it tastes very good. If it's like this tomorrow, and still like this the day after tomorrow, we will feel it's tasteless. The love between husband and wife drops from boiling point to freezing point, which is the same principle. (2) We must advocate "Husband and Wife Sunday Meetings," that is, the husband and wife live apart. Every Sunday, the two agree on a location to meet, and after this day, they each go to work separately.

Mr. Dai Kejian's message: (1) Approximately five reasons: (1) incompatible personalities, (2) the other person is ugly, (3) difficult living conditions, (4) the husband is unfaithful, or the wife is gluttonous and lazy, (5) after having children, the children divide the husband's love. (2) Must accept fate, must forgive each other, must be able to live in peace in wealth, and stick together in poverty.

(2) A Letter That Can Be Used as a Reference for Ms. Zhang Yunqiu

Ms. Shi Ziwo's message: I have only been married for four years and have very little experience. I am not qualified to participate in the discussion of the major issue of love after marriage raised by Ms. Zhang Yunqiu. However, my experience is completely opposite to that of Ms. Zhang, and I have already passed the critical stage (i.e., one or two years of marriage), so I am willing to contribute my own experience to the public. My husband was initially introduced by my father. When we first met, it wasn't like what people say, "love at first sight." Although he is only five years older than me, his appearance is older than his age, especially when he frowns and thinks. Therefore, I said to my father, "He could be my old uncle." But my father liked him very much and said many words praising him. To please my father, I reluctantly arranged a time to talk with him. Who knew that after talking, my impression of him changed, and I felt that he was a rare "comrade" of mine. His views and thoughts were completely the same as mine. It wasn't that he deliberately accommodated my meaning; at that time, I was just asking questions; he answered. We talked several times, gradually developing love from respect, and becoming a couple from respect and love. We believe that our love now is stronger and sweeter than when we got married four years ago. As for how to achieve a happy result, it is difficult to explain in detail, but analyzing it, there are several principles. Marriage is related to lifelong happiness. When we got married, we decided to do our best to make our life happy, just like what Shanghainese call "being husband and wife." We never thought, what if married life fails? If there is any dissatisfaction, we will try to resolve it frankly and not let the situation escalate.

I never compare my husband with others, because such comparisons are harmful and not beneficial.

Married life is very different from life before marriage, especially in terms of sexual desire. We were prepared for this change in life. We completely followed the guidance of the Englishman Stopes. We both carefully read his book "Married Love" (Marie Stopes: Married Love, there is a translated version of this book on the market), and we discussed all the questions raised in the book.

We both try our best to avoid all things that cause jealousy or misunderstanding. Even so, small disagreements between husband and wife sometimes occur. There was a time when we argued almost every day. Later, we agreed that neither of us should lose our temper. After that, when a disagreement occurred, we would say, "Didn't we agree not to lose our temper?" Once this was said, neither of us wanted to continue arguing. Another method is to understand each other. I want to believe that if he loses his temper, he is not losing it at me, he still loves me, maybe he was upset by someone outside, or he is not feeling well: I should comfort him. He treats me the same way. When women are menstruating, their tempers are irritable, and they often become pessimistic over trivial matters; so when we encounter menstruation, we pay special attention. With this in mind, if the other person says something unreasonable, we don't dwell on it. If I am unhappy and want to lose my temper, I will try my best to think of all the good things about the other person and try to restrain myself. If I really can't restrain myself, I will go to bed earlier, or go to friends and relatives to play, which are all ways to avoid losing my temper. My husband usually pays close attention to my temperament, so when I get angry, he can make me laugh. We both pay attention not to offend what the other person dislikes. For example, he hates others wronging him the most. Regarding this, I pay attention to avoid it. He often praises me, making me embarrassed to do things that displease him; this is also his method.

Regarding household affairs, the responsibilities of both of us are very clear.

Economically, my husband is fully responsible, but I am not wasteful either, and I follow the budget for expenses. There was a time when our family finances were very difficult. He was able to calculate, live within our means, and not be in debt; therefore, many difficult problems were reduced. I must discuss major family matters with my husband, but he does not ask about daily matters at all. If the servants make mistakes, he does not directly blame them, but only tells me. I absolutely do not interfere in his work matters; because I know that if I interfere, it will not help, but will make it more difficult for him to handle things.

We already have children, but I will never neglect my husband because of raising children, so that when he comes home from work, he cannot get the happiness of the family. We also have a certain policy for educating children. When we encounter rewards and punishments, we must agree before proceeding.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong and the coastal areas of the country, the weather is clear and cold, gradually becoming cloudy, with strong seasonal winds, coming from the northwest to the northeast, etc. The Yangtze River basin is cold and cloudy, and the northwest wind is still moderate. The center of one was within 60 miles of the intersection of 19 degrees north latitude and 125 degrees east longitude at around 6:00 AM. One at noon advanced within 60 miles of the intersection of 28 degrees latitude north and 138 degrees east longitude, with strong winds. Shanghai Northeast Refugee Relief Association

Urgent Announcement Regarding Monthly Donation Campaign

More than a year has passed since the Northeast fell. The whole country is silent, relying solely on the volunteer army to fight desperately. The dead lie in corpses in the borderlands, and the living bathe in blood in the icy sky. If we do not expand relief and provide long-term assistance, the volunteer army will be destroyed and the Northeast will be lost, and China will also be lost. Therefore, based on the purpose of saving people and saving ourselves, we have publicly discussed the monthly donation method.

(1) This monthly donation is limited to six months. (2) The Northeast Refugee Relief Association is established in Peiping as the central organization for Northeast relief, presided over by General Zhu Ziqiao. All donations from this association will be remitted to it for allocation. (3) Office expenses are borne entirely by the initiators, and no donations will be used at all. (4) Collection agencies: 1. Major banks in this port; 2. Hengxun, Fuyuan, Tongchun, Qingcheng, Yida five money shops; 3. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce.

Peiping-Tientsin Education Association Prepares to Clear Accumulated Tuition Fees

Peiping, 7th - The Peiping-Tientsin Education Association is preparing to clear the accumulated tuition fees from the government over the years. Peking University, Normal University, and other schools are issuing a list of accumulated debts.

Ministry of Education Explains Examination Regulations

(Vocational and Normal Subjects Temporarily Exempt from Examination)

The Ministry of Education, according to the Hubei Provincial Department of Education's request for interpretation of the high school graduation examination regulations, generally means that according to the high school graduation examination regulations, junior high, high school, and high school general subjects should hold daily examinations. In addition, such as junior high vocational subjects and high school normal subjects, whether they also need to hold examinations, and all subjects in the examination pass, but the subjects not in the examination fail, whether they are allowed to graduate, and whether the graduation grade is calculated by averaging the grades of all subjects in the examination and the subjects not in the examination, the Ministry of Education instructed the Department as follows on the 6th: (1) Vocational and normal subjects are temporarily exempt from examination. (2) Those who pass all subjects in the examination and fail in subjects not in the examination, but whose overall average score still passes, are allowed to graduate. (3) The overall graduation grade should be calculated by totaling the grades of all subjects in the examination and the grades of subjects not in the examination.

The Ministry of Education has compiled statistics on national libraries in the 19th year, and the following is an excerpt of its summary: The nature of the libraries is divided into (1) ordinary, (2) specialized, (3) public, (4) attached to social education institutions, (5) attached to institutions and organizations, (6) newspaper and magazine outlets, (7) schools, (8) private collections. The Initiation of the Jiangsu Provincial Primary School Federation

Decision Made by Principals of Experimental Primary Schools and Directors of Attached Primary Schools

The principals of Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Primary Schools and the directors of attached primary schools held a meeting at the attached primary school of Zhenjiang Normal School at 1:00 PM on the 6th of this month. A total of 16 schools, including the attached primary school of Wuxi Normal School, arrived. Shen Shanzhi, director of the attached primary school of Zhenjiang Normal School, was elected as the temporary chairman, and Pan Ren, director of the attached primary school of Wuxi Normal School, recorded the minutes. After the ceremony, the chairman first reported the significance of the meeting. Shi Renfu of Jiangsu Primary School reported on the general situation of the former Experimental Primary School Federation. Ma Ketan of Nanjing Central Experimental Primary School reported on the provincial funding situation. Guo Xinong of Xuzhou Central Experimental Primary School reported on the progress of the liaison for Boy Scout subsidies. Then, the cases were discussed and resolved: (1) Organize the Provincial Experimental Primary School Federation. The new board of directors will draft the constitution based on the following points: A. Organize the board of directors to handle the affairs of this association. B. Schools with less than five grades in this association will pay an annual membership fee of 5 yuan, schools with less than ten grades will pay 10 yuan, and schools with more than ten grades will pay 15 yuan. C. The task of this association is limited to jointly seeking the development of school affairs and studying ongoing matters. D. This association will hold an annual meeting once a year and hold board meetings twice per semester, and convene ad hoc meetings when necessary. (2) Continue to carry out the Jiangsu Children's Airplane Savings Fund. The board of directors will supervise the progress. (3) Send a letter to the Provincial Education Funding Management Office, requesting that the December funding be paid out by January 10th. Ma Ketan of Nanjing Central Primary School and Shen Zishan of Nanjing Women's Central Primary School were assigned to be responsible for liaison. (4) Submit to the Provincial Party Department of Education, requesting that primary schools be subsidized 60 yuan per grade per year according to the standard for Boy Scout subsidies for provincial high schools. (5) The attached primary schools of this association will jointly submit a request to the Education Department to increase the funding for the attached primary schools of rural teachers' schools, and allocate it according to the standard of the attached primary schools of normal schools. (6) The first annual meeting of this association is scheduled to be held in Nantong in early May next year, and at the same time, the achievements of "Civic Training" will be exhibited. Finally, the attached primary school of Zhenjiang Normal School, the Nanjing Central Experimental Primary School, the Nanjing Women's Central Experimental Primary School, the Jiangsu Central Experimental Primary School, and the attached primary school of Wuxi Normal School were elected as directors, and the Shanghai Central Experimental Primary School and the Yangzhou Central Experimental Primary School were elected as alternate directors. The attached primary school of Zhenjiang Normal School was designated as the chief director until 4:00 PM when the meeting adjourned.

Ministry of Education Promulgates Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum Standards (60)

Music

First, Objectives

(1) To conform to children's happy and lively nature, so as to develop their interest and talent in appreciating and applying music.

(2) To develop children's ability to hear and vocalize.

(3) To cultivate children's emotions such as love and courage, and to encourage their spirit of unity and progress.

Second, Types of Assignments

(1) Appreciation: (1) Appreciation of vocal music: Appreciation of domestic and foreign popular songs, solos and choruses. (2) Appreciation of instrumental music: Appreciation of domestic and foreign popular instruments, solos and ensembles.

(2) Practice: (1) Listening practice: Practice in distinguishing the pitch, length, and intervals of sounds, and melodies. (2) Vocalization practice: Practice in vocalizing head tones, throat tones, high and low pitches, and long and short sounds. (3) Song solo and chorus: Singing and chorus practice of songs and children's operas. (4) Expression practice: Expression of songs and role-playing in operas. (5) Music score copying: Dictation and copying of simple monophonic scores. (6) Instrument playing: Selection and practice of organs and various common instruments in the country.

(3) Research: (1) Music score recognition: Recognition of ordinary music scores (limited to staff, notes, rests, key signatures, scales, intervals, and various symbols of loudness, tempo, and abbreviation that are commonly used). (2) Study of singing methods: Study of various vocalization and singing methods. (3) Study of performance methods: Study of methods for expressing songs. (4) Study of instrument playing methods: Study of the playing methods of various instruments. (5) Study of instrument construction and repair methods: Study of the construction and simple repair methods of ordinary instruments.

(Note) The research questions arise from the difficulties or needs felt during appreciation and practice, so research should be integrated with appreciation and practice, and should not be taught separately. However, it can be appropriately changed in the fifth and sixth grades.

Third, Key Assignments for Each School Year

Appreciation Practice Research Notes

First and Second Grades

1. Appreciation of songs that children find pleasant and noble.

2. Appreciation of the performance of common musical instruments that children find pleasant.

3. Listening, singing, and performing games with lyrics in colloquial style that are rich in movement and children's literature.

4. Listening exercises for various group imitation movements.

5. Practice of two types of time signatures.

6. Distinguishing sounds.

7. Vocalization methods.

8. Distinguishing the pitch and length of sounds.

9. Expression and performance methods.

Weekly Time

90 minutes (divided into three sessions)

Third and Fourth Grades

1. 2. Continue items 1 and 2 from the previous school year.

2. Appreciation of the performance or ensemble of common musical instruments in China and abroad.

3. Sight-singing and performance of lyrics in colloquial style that are rich in movement and children's literature.

4. Role-playing in children's operas.

5. Continue item 6 from the previous school year and add practice in time signatures.

6. Recognition of C and G keys and various notes such as quarter notes, half notes, eighth notes, whole notes, and rests.

7. Sight-singing of single-tone songs in C and G keys (when singing, it is still advisable to use keys suitable for children's nature such as D major, C major, E major, F major, etc. The solfège can adopt the fixed solfège method).

8. Continue items 7 and 8 from the previous school year. 10. Method of copying music scores.

Weekly Time

90 minutes (divided into three sessions)

Fifth and Sixth Grades

1. 2. 3. Continue items 1, 2, and 3 from the previous school year.

2. Appreciation of musical style and interest.

3. Appreciation of famous Chinese songs (such as Yuequ Pingdiao, etc.) and foreign famous songs (such as folk songs of various countries, etc.).

4. Sight-singing and expression of lyrics that are rich in emotion and thought.

5. Role-playing in children's operas.

6. Continue item from the previous school year and add practice in time signatures.

7. Recognition of various keys such as C, G, and F, and sixteenth notes, rests, dotted notes, and various symbols such as # and b.

8. Sight-singing practice of easy monophonic songs, two-part round songs, and two-part harmony songs.

9. Copying and dictation of music scores.

10. Selection and practice of organs and various common instruments in the country.

11. The relationship between songs and music.

12. The main points of music score organization.

13. Common sense of Chinese and foreign music and music stories.

Weekly Time

90 minutes (divided into three sessions)

1. The arrangement of music time should be after the homework that is used, and should not be arranged after physical education. However, the first and second grades can often be linked with physical education games for teaching; each grade can also be linked with dance for teaching.

2. The fixed solfège method is to fix do as C, re as D, mi as E, fa as F, so as G, la as A, and si as B. No matter how the key changes, its solfège remains fixed. Even the sharps and flats caused by the change of key still follow the fixed solfège method and are fixed.

Fourth, Teaching Points

In the first year of elementary school, the teaching is entirely based on the listening-singing method (emphasis on listening and singing the lyrics; the music score can be listened to more but not sung). The lyrics taught are best performed to increase children's interest.

Second, In the second and third grades of elementary school, the period is a transition from listening and singing to sight-singing, still focusing on sight-singing and performing the lyrics. If children understand the value of musical symbols and need to learn, they can use charts, cards, gestures, and other varied and interesting methods to instruct.

Third, In the fourth year of elementary school, focus on sight-singing teaching. When teaching new lyrics, children can make clear learning of simple music scores. The modes and uses of Chinese and foreign musical instruments, and the ways and uses of ancient and modern ethnic groups' expressions of interest in music can all be started to guide.

Fourth, As far as possible, use the sight-singing method for teaching. If there are songs that can be performed, they must still be performed. The way the music score is organized, the purpose and effectiveness of each method must be understood by the children.

Fifth, Often link teaching with language literature, social studies (such as the musical design of various eras and ethnic groups), work (such as occupational songs of farmers and workers), hygiene, and other designs. In particular, it should be used for the needs of social events, seasonal gatherings, etc. and taught appropriate songs.

Sixth, Music scores should use materials that conform to the national character as much as possible, but mainly use materials that are happy, lively, brave, solemn, and varied. Materials that are sad, negative, and oily or dull and rigid should be avoided.

Seventh, Lyrics should be children's literature, mainly to encourage children's movements, to invigorate personal feelings, and to promote the national spirit. Do not use exhortations or maxims as materials.

Eighth, When teaching new songs, in addition to simple music scores, teachers should often sing and play music as an example so that children can listen. To avoid confusing hearing, it is best not to use musical instrument accompaniment when singing as an example.

Ninth, Children should be made to sing the songs faithfully, and it is strictly forbidden to arbitrarily add embellishments or shout loudly. After each song is practiced, children should be encouraged to sing solos.

Tenth, Within the possible scope, make full use of record players and various local opportunities to listen to music, and teach methods for appreciating music.

Eleventh, Regarding the teaching of appreciation, in addition to specially selected appreciation teaching materials, attention should also be paid to appreciating the songs sung during practice.

Twelfth, Teachers' attitudes should pay attention to neatness and amiability, and their voice skills should pay more attention to beauty and skill. At the beginning of each music teaching, use stories and questions that inspire emotions to arouse children's motivation to learn.

Thirteenth, Teachers should correct children's postures, and pay special attention to them during development.

Fourteenth, When necessary, breathing should be performed as a preparation for singing, and sound should be practiced to ensure accurate singing. When practicing sound, use various changing methods to make children not tired, such as imitating bird calls, insect calls, wind sounds, kite sounds, baby cries, or compiling interesting sentences for children to answer.

Fifteenth, The teaching of lyrics should make children first understand the meaning of the lyrics. The teacher should fully imply the feelings of the lyrics with their attitude (for example, joy is joyful, sorrow is sorrowful, solemnity is solemn, humor is humorous).

Sixteenth, New knowledge of music scores should be constantly compared and studied with old knowledge. For example, the similarities and differences between quarter notes and eighth notes, the differences in the positions of each scale in the G key and C key on the staff... all must be compared to make children understand.

Seventeenth, The practice of songs should be varied in one time, such as singing sometimes, practicing sound sometimes, listening to music sometimes, performing sometimes, shouting section sometimes, dancing section sometimes, clapping section sometimes, standing singing sometimes, sitting sometimes, walking singing sometimes, singing in unison sometimes, singing solo sometimes, singing in groups sometimes... the methods are not the same.

Eighteenth, Attention should be paid to children's range, vocal area, and breathing and vocalization. If there are children with a single tone, their seats should be in the front row or next to the teacher, with special training, and pay attention to them at all times, not letting him hinder the beautiful and pure singing of the whole grade.

Nineteenth, Children should stop singing during the period of voice change, and more practice lessons should be used to replace them in theoretical aspects.

Twentieth, Within the possible scope, encourage children to create and apply songs at any time (such as gatherings, festivals, etc.) (such as using skilled music scores to create lyrics, etc.) to develop children's talent for expressing emotions with music.

Twenty-first, Schools should encourage children to learn various musical instruments and should organize bands, opera performances, music competitions, etc.

Twenty-second, The musical instruments used should be mainly organs or violins. In schools with a lack of funding, the Xiao, flute, and Huqin can be used for teaching.

Twenty-third, The music score should be a staff, and simplified notation should not be used unless absolutely necessary. It is absolutely forbidden to use simplified notation together with staff notation for teaching.

Twenty-fourth, Hearing training should be given special attention. Therefore, the "fixed solfège method" (which is the same-tone singing method commonly used by European and Latin nations) can be adopted for the singing method of the staff, but because of the lack of teachers, the non-fixed solfège method (which is the different-tone singing method commonly used by countries such as the United Kingdom and the United States) can still be adopted. It is also a trend for British and Americans to use same-tone singing.

Twenty-fifth, Within the possible scope, various Chinese and foreign musical instruments should be prepared, and a classroom specially designed for music teaching should be set up.

Educational Delegation Arrives in London

Three Weeks of Observation in England

London, December 6th, Reuters - The Chinese Education Observation Group, including Cheng Qibao, arrived here today from Europe and plans to stay in England for three weeks. This afternoon, they will attend a reception at Isang Hsia's residence. Tomorrow, they will visit various educational and cultural institutions in Oxford. On Friday, they will go to Cambridge. Two days later, they will go to Eire [Ireland]. They are scheduled to return to London on the 11th, at which time they will confer with education officials and attend a luncheon at the House of Commons at the invitation of former Indian Governor Lord Irwin. On other days, they will be guided by members of the London County Council to visit various schools managed by the council. On December 18th, Cheng and others will go to Leeds to visit rural schools, followed by Wakefield and Reading for observation. After completing their observations, they will be hosted at a banquet by the Chinese Legation on December 23rd.

Ministry of Education Orders Shandong Education Department to Hold Screening Exams for High School Lower Semester

丨Principal Song Huanwu Resigns, Retained丨

Jinan, December 7th - The Ministry of Education telegraphed Director of Education He Siyuan, stating that high school students had defied orders and gone on strike, and that persuasion had been ineffective. The department ordered the school to be dissolved and the case prepared. Principal Song Erwu's resignation has been retained.

Municipal Education Bureau to Hold Health Speech Contest for Primary and Secondary Schools

Preliminary Rounds to Begin on the 20th of This Month, Finals to be Held on the 28th

In order to enhance students' health and intelligence, and to train their speaking skills, the Municipal Education Bureau is holding a city-wide health speech contest for primary and secondary schools, divided into high school, junior high school, and elementary school groups. All municipal and registered private primary and secondary schools may participate. The dates for the preliminary rounds have been set: the 20th of this month for the areas of Huinan Yinxiang, Jiangwan, and Caojing; the 21st for Zhabei, Pengpu, Zhenru, Yangsi, and the First Special District; the 22nd for Yinhang, Pusong, Tangqiao, Yangjing, and Gaohang; and the 23rd for Wusong, Fahua, Luhang, Gaoqiao, and the Second Special District. The preliminary rounds will be held at venues designated by the Municipal Education Bureau in each district. Representatives selected from the preliminary rounds will participate in the semi-finals at 1:00 PM on December 26th. Twelve students from the high school and junior high school groups, and twenty-five students from the elementary school group, will be selected as finalists to participate in the finals at 1:00 PM on the 28th. The final locations are Wumu Girls' School for the high school group, He'an Elementary School for the junior high school group, and the Municipal People's Education Center for the elementary school group. Speech times for the preliminary and semi-final rounds are eight minutes per person for high school and junior high school students, and four minutes per person for elementary school students. Speech times for the finals are ten minutes per person for high school and junior high school students, and five minutes per person for elementary school students. All speeches must be delivered in Mandarin Chinese. The theme of the speeches should be related to health education, and students should choose their own topics, but the topic for the preliminary round must be the same as for the semi-final and final rounds. The Municipal Education Bureau will hire experts to serve as judges. Five individual awards will be given to the high school group and ten to the elementary school group, each receiving a medal. Three school awards will be given to each group, each receiving a certificate.

Liangjiang Controls Meifu and Chongde's Failure Was a Pity

In last night's Western Girls' Basketball League games, Liangjiang and Southeast successively defeated their opponents, but because the opponents' strengths varied, the situations differed accordingly. The ease with which they won was also different. Liangjiang had a smooth run, reaching the realm of victory directly, while Southeast faced repeated risks, and its victory was not easy to come by. Initially, the Blue Team gained little due to Liangjiang's strong defense, but later Liangjiang's formation became disorganized, and the Blue Team launched a large-scale invasion. As a result, the Blue Team won with nineteen to nine.

Hangzhou Sports World

Inviting Famous Sports Athletes and Groups from Shanghai to Perform in Hangzhou in the New Year

(Football: Donghua and Jinan Teams)

(Basketball: Chizhi and Jinan Teams)

(Volleyball: Fudan and Jinan Teams)

(Tennis: Qiu Feihai, Lin Baohua, etc.)

In recent years, Zhejiang Province's sports cause has been promoted by the education authorities, and people from all walks of life have gradually paid attention to various ball games, and are very interested in holding them. However, there are no strong enemies to compete with in the inland, and there is a lack of experience. Except for the volleyball skills of the Art College, which are somewhat remarkable, the combat capabilities of other teams are weak. Free Talk

Short Story

The Capture of Square Fort (1)

— French American Star Film Translation

A soldier, who died of heatstroke in Greece a few years ago, once told me about his first combat experience. I was deeply moved by the story, so I later took the time to write it down from memory. Here is the story:

× × × ×

I returned to my unit on the afternoon of September 4th. I met the regimental commander in the camp. He was initially quite rude to me, but after reading General B's letter of recommendation, his expression changed, and he exchanged a few polite words with me.

He introduced me to the squadron commander, who had just returned from an inspection. This squadron commander, whom I later had no time to get to know, was a tall, chestnut-haired man with a stern and unpleasant face. He had previously been a private, and he had earned his epaulettes and cross on the battlefield. His voice was hoarse and low, not at all in proportion to his huge body. I was told that his strange voice was a gift from a bullet that had pierced him during the Battle of Eylau.

When he heard that I was from the Fontainebleau Artillery School, he made an ugly face and said:

丨My lieutenant died yesterday...

I knew he meant to say, "You are the one to fill his vacancy, but you are not worthy of the job." I wanted to retort with a sharp remark, but I held back.

The moon rose from behind the Square Fort of Sevastopol, which was separated from our camp by two cannon shots. It was large and red, just as it usually rose. But that night, it seemed particularly large to me. For a moment, the square fort stood out as a distinct black silhouette against a backdrop of brilliant moonlight. It looked like the cone of an erupting volcano. An old soldier next to me noticed the color of the moon.

丨The moon is very red, he said; this means that this famous square fort will require many sacrifices to capture!

I have always been very superstitious, especially at this time, and this omen could not help but move me. I went to sleep, but I couldn't fall asleep. I got up and walked around for a while, looking at the vast front line that enveloped the hills opposite the village of Sevastopol.

When I felt that the cool evening air was enough to calm my blood, I returned to the fire; I carefully wrapped myself in my cloak, closed my eyes, and hoped not to open them again until dawn. But sleep never came. My thoughts unconsciously sank into a state of sorrow. I thought to myself that among the hundred thousand people who filled the plains, I did not have a single friend, and if I were injured, I would sleep in a hospital, neglected by some ignorant surgeons. Many stories I had heard about surgery surged into my memory. My heart beat violently, and I mechanically adjusted the handkerchief and pouch hanging on my chest like a kind of armor. I was too tired to bear it, and I dozed off from time to time, but I was always awakened by a powerful, ominous thought. But fatigue finally prevailed, and when the morning drums began to beat, I fell fast asleep. We lined up, took roll call, and then we stacked our guns in bundles, all of which foreshadowed a quiet day for us.

At three o'clock, an adjutant arrived with an order. We were again ordered to take up arms; our skirmishers spread out across the plain, and we slowly advanced behind them. Twenty minutes later, we saw all of the Russian soldiers' outposts retreating back into the square fort.

On Dwelling

— Man

The universe is originally a large house. People come with cries and leave with smiles, all like passing guests in a dream. Precisely because they are passers-by, they must enjoy this moment of time to the fullest before taking their last breath. Even if they do not plan for future generations, from one generation to the next to ten thousand generations, they should at least have a piece of land where they can stand firmly. This is where the issue of "dwelling" arises.

As most people think, the heavens and the earth are so vast that anywhere can be a home. Moreover, from cave dwelling to the present day, red walls and green tiles have almost covered the five continents and ten thousand countries. Even if grandchildren are born from children, and the population grows day by day, who would believe that they cannot find a place to live?

However, things are not so simple. Look at those who live in dilapidated walls, exposed to wind and sun, those who stand like doves and cranes, relying on others for shelter, those who take refuge in open spaces, using the sky as a brocade and the earth as a carpet, exposed to wind and rain, they are all before our eyes, numbering far more than just thousands and thousands. As the saying goes, "Having no land to stand on when alive and no place to be buried when dead," can this heaven and earth truly be considered "vast"?

But on the other hand, there are also the palaces of Afang with a building every five steps and a pavilion every ten steps, with rows of brocade curtains stretching forty miles long. Take, for example, the Forbidden City in Beijing, with its winding corridors and numerous palaces and halls. There are also rooms with carpets, marble floors, small gardens, large kitchens, plus a few mansions and villas, all just for "dwelling." Comparing the group who "have no land to stand on when alive" with the group who live in the palaces of Afang, although we do not want to emulate Liu Bang and sigh, "Should a true man not be like this?" but this vast house of the universe belongs to everyone. Since everyone is like a passing guest in a dream, then to forcibly call a portion of people homeless, while another portion "gets what they want, gets what they want," then at least a flaw has occurred in this world! Alas, "When can we get a great mansion of ten thousand rooms, to shelter all the poor scholars of the world and make them smile with joy!"

× × × ×

To the Children

— Biyun

My dear Inge, my little darling:

Naturally, it was out of boredom that I took out all the letters from friends from the drawer and flipped through them page by page. Behind your mother's letter, I found a few words of your greetings, and I immediately thought of writing you a letter. Although my handwriting is scribbled and there are many things I say that you do not understand, your mother will read it to you and explain it to you better than I can write. Little darling, as long as you understand one-third of what I say, I will be satisfied, and the mission of this letter will be accomplished. Dear child, take a good look at this letter.

Today is a rainy day. It is said that Japan is always like this, with very few sunny days. At first, I did not believe it, but after living here for twenty days, it really proved that what they said was true. In these twenty days, I have only seen the sun twice and the moon once, but in less than three hours, it became cloudy again. The sky is filled with gloomy and miserable clouds, symbolizing the future of Japanese imperialism with a deathly stillness.

People living in this kind of climate are most prone to complaining, especially someone like me who grew up in the intensely sunny South. Living this kind of life is really painful. I am sad, my heart is just itchy, and it feels like something wants to jump out of my eyes, but a minute passes, and that thing still hasn't come out. I know it is being suppressed by reason, because if it came out, this letter might not be written.

Today is the Double Tenth Festival, and your school must be closed. You may be sitting next to your mother reading, playing with a toy gun, or staring blankly at the sky. If Shanghai is raining like it is here, then you must be even more unhappy, because you can't go out to play, and your mother wants to write more things on a rainy day. She not only won't take you to play or tell you stories, but she will also forbid you from speaking, forbid you from singing, and even interfere with your slightest movement. Alas, poor child, I am worried about you. If Shanghai is raining today like it is here, then how will you get through it? Are you as bored as I am?

I don't know why, but there are very few times when I forget about children. This is not because I have a child of my own, but because I have always liked children. Because I feel that only children are innocent, pure, and loyal. They have no hypocrisy, no pride, and no base or cruel behavior. They have no class consciousness. If the children of wealthy families are not good, it is because their families have taught them badly. The "Three Character Classic" says, "At the beginning of man, his nature is good," and that is indeed true!

Inge, you are indeed too pitiful! The children in the same alley as you are all happier than you. They have toy cars, dolls, beautiful clothes and hats, and in winter, they have coats and velvet hats, and they take chauffeured cars to school, with nannies picking them up and dropping them off... But you can't even get enough to eat sometimes. Occasionally, you steal two copper coins from your mother to buy candy, and you get a beating when you come back. Do you remember? Dear little darling! That was three days before I left the country. Your mother came to invite me and another friend to dinner. I knew she couldn't afford to treat, so we bought four eggs to bring with us, but later, those eggs were never cooked. It turned out that there was already a bowl of dried tofu stir-fried with diced meat, cabbage, and shrimp and radish soup on the table. "Is there enough food?" Your mother asked us with a shy smile.

"Enough, enough, of course, enough!" This was our reply to her.

Even now, I still want to ask you, little darling, when exactly were those four eggs cooked and eaten? How many did you eat? Did your mother beat you?

Alas! Speaking of beating, I really feel sorry for you! It was that time when we were eating at your house that your mother, because you were eating too much food, hurriedly used chopsticks to hit your soft, plump, bun-like little hand a few times. We were very upset for you and blamed her for being so violent. She replied to us very seriously: "You don't know, he only eats vegetables every day. When he eats too much salt, he drinks water like crazy. This is not only harmful to his health, but it also makes him buy boiling water many times a day!"

Alas! Little darling, do you know? It is not easy for your mother to even get the money to buy boiling water! She is constantly holding a pen and writing, sometimes sighing, sometimes crying, and sometimes laughing and crying like a madwoman. Little darling, this is all because the oppression of life has led to such mental pain and such abnormality!

This letter stops here. After I receive your reply, I will say other things.

I wish you and your little friends who share the same fate to be lively and happy!

Life Exhausted, Pulse Severed

— Zifang

"Education is the lifeblood of the nation," this "new" cliché seems to have been heard by us for a long time; a very long time. However, what we see with our own eyes is either the education funds of a certain province or a certain province's primary schools have not been distributed for several months, or the teachers and staff of a certain middle school are making trouble in the hall, demanding arrears, or a certain university has formally suspended operations due to a lack of funds.

Under this educational crisis in which arrears of salaries and a lack of food have become widespread, students have become wandering elements with nowhere to go, and nineteen out of ten teachers and staff have become poor victims suffering from a lack of clothing and food. If "education is the lifeblood of the nation" is a true statement, then our old and sick country has indeed reached a stage where its life is exhausted and its pulse is severed!

Science

Television

— He

Television is a scientific invention that broadcasts sound and images simultaneously using the principles of radio. Its English name is Television, and the Japanese translation is テレビ (terebi).

The speech and music broadcast from a distant broadcasting station are transmitted through radio waves and amplified by the receiver's amplifier, allowing you to hear the same speech or music as the broadcasting station. This is radio broadcasting. Because this can only hear sound, it is "radio for the ears."

Then, what I want to talk about here is radio broadcasting of images, which is the so-called "radio for the eyes." For example, if the broadcasting station is performing the Peking opera "Si Lang Visits His Mother," after the radio waves are transmitted, the Television receivers in all directions will show people the movements of the actors and listen to the singing, just like opening a sound movie.

Due to space limitations, the structure of television transmitters and receivers cannot be explained in detail. The principle is summarized as follows.

For example, when Mei Lanfang is singing "Su San Starts Her Journey" at the broadcasting station, his posture becomes a small photograph through a spherical lens. However, after passing through the Nipkow disk, the image is projected onto a photocell. The photocell converts light into electricity, which is then sent to the transmitter and becomes radio waves. Finally, it is broadcast by the antenna. That's the broadcasting aspect.

Next, I will explain the receiver. The radio waves received by the antenna are introduced into the amplifier of the television receiver, and then introduced into a device that changes the degree of brightness by passing electricity through light. Then, due to the strong light, different intensities of light are displayed actively on the white cloth, and Mei Lanfang's posture in the distance is faintly smiling before our eyes. As for the transmission and reception of sound, it is the broadcasting and receiving of sound by radio: converting sound into radio waves, emitting it from the antenna, and then receiving the radio waves from the antenna, repeating the process of converting it back into sound and amplifying it for transmission.

Because the sound and image are transmitted simultaneously on that side, and the sound and image are received simultaneously on this side, it is like watching a sound movie at home.

Regarding this science, countries are still competing to continue research, and it can be said that it is still in the experimental stage. Undoubtedly, the application of Television is extremely broad. Russia has been working hard to implement it in recent years, making its devices common in rural areas, and it has become a powerful tool for public education.

Long Novel

The Crossroads of Time and Love 8

— Zhang Ziping

As she was about to go downstairs, she turned her head to look at Jinhua and said with a smile. "...Rest assured, right?"

"Not at ease."

"Well, then I won't go down. I'll wait for you to go down together."

She deliberately stopped her footsteps.

"She's having some kind of free love affair with your sister. She must be a modern youth. You have to be careful. Be careful when you speak, don't let him laugh at you."

"What free love, I'm tired of hearing these words. None of the marriages based on free love have good results. Our marriage is still happy, the order of parents, the words of a matchmaker. We didn't know each other before, so what's wrong with that?"

"But, our marriage is barbaric. From the perspective of those modern youths, locking up men and women who don't know each other in a room... is a sin...."

"Don't talk nonsense again!"

"So we are all guilty of sin."

"I won't listen, I won't listen."

"The attitude of Peizhen on the first night... Ha, ha, ha!"

Peizhen stretched out her hands to cover her ears and went downstairs. Jinhua didn't stop laughing until she couldn't see her. He heard his wife whistling as she went down the escalator step by step. She was singing something like a dance tune.

Haiquan saw the sister of his lover, and what shocked him was that Peizhen's facial features and the configuration of her eyebrows, eyes, nose, and mouth were more beautiful than her sister's. Following this shock, his whole body also felt a slight tremor, and his voice trembled unexpectedly when he answered her. He gradually saw the differences between the sisters. The older sister's figure was more sensual, while the younger sister's figure was too thin. The older sister's face was rounder, while the younger sister's face was a bit pointed. The older sister's expression was cheerful, while the younger sister's expression was melancholy. The older sister's attitude was emotional, while the younger sister's attitude was rational.

He felt that Peizhen was not as arrogant as the rumors said. She asked him many questions about Guangdong. Finally, she also told him to come and play often, just like with his own family.

After a moment, that Master Ren also came down to greet him. Haiquan only felt that he was a complete American returnee. When he spoke, he inserted a few English words from time to time. Haiquan heard the word "Sure" countless times. His hands were in his trouser pockets, and he shrugged his shoulders every time he said a joke.

"Why do people outside say that they are arrogant? Aren't they very kind and approachable people?"

Haiquan thought again that maybe it was only like this to him. Because he had family ties with them.

Haiquan originally wanted to say goodbye after sitting for a while. But after seeing this Master Ren's wife, he didn't want to leave. After talking with her for a while, he felt even more that she had a charm that made people want to stay.

He finally had lunch at their house. It was already after three o'clock when he said goodbye to the Ren family. Master Ren even specially called a car to send him back to Professor Zeng's house in Beiqiaobei.

The Gold Market in Financial Turmoil

(Finally Fell Another One or Two Taels) Yesterday's market continued to decline slightly, although there was a state of drifting, there was no major storm. The difference between the high and low points of the overall market was less than six taels, and finally it fell another one or two taels. The market opened weakly, presumably due to the rise in the silver market, the rise in forward prices, and the continued rise in exchange rates. In the future, due to the overt and covert flattening of bills of exchange, there will be both good and bad quality at times, and due to the different disbursements of various parties, the price of gold often fluctuates by two or three taels. However, it always hovers within 800 taels, and people's minds are inevitably confused. Since the market is closed on Wednesday, the detailed situation of the half-day will be recorded later.

(Hovering within the 800 Taels Mark) From the opening of the market in January at 795 taels and a half, it immediately fell by one tael and three mace. Shortly afterwards, Dadaicheng, Yifengyong, and Wupin and others came in, and the US dollar against one, two, and three months was only settled at 31.25. China-Belgium absorbed British gold at 25 for April, so the gold price rose by four taels. At 9:30, it was 98 taels and 8 mace. New Prices Suddenly Appear for Foreign Interest

丨Exceeding the 4% Threshold丨

Yesterday, foreign exchange transactions were firm due to another large export volume in the afternoon. Silver taels, however, remained in a weak state. As for settlement news, banks remained relatively strong, while money shops, with the end of the year approaching and the time for settlements drawing near, mostly reduced their activity.

(Interest Rises, Discount Softens) The morning market for "foreign interest" was at 7 mace, 1 fen, 3 li, 7 hao, 5 si, the same as the previous day's afternoon market. The afternoon market suddenly rose by another 3 hao, 7 hu, 5 si, exceeding the 4% threshold, with 7 mace, 1 fen, 4 li, 1 hao, 2 hu, 5 si, reappearing at the new high price of the first half of the year. The "silver discount" was the same in both the morning and afternoon markets, at 3% plus water, with no market and uniformly white.

(Copper Coins Continue to Shrink) Jiangnan small foreign coins were at 6 mace, 2 fen, 5 li in the morning market and 6 mace, 2 fen, 8 li in the afternoon market. The transaction volume was 6,000 jiao in the morning market and 9,500 jiao in the afternoon market. Guangdong small foreign coins were at 6 mace, 2 fen, 3 li, 5 hao in the morning market, with the same price in the afternoon market. The transaction volume was 110,000 jiao in the morning market and 30,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins shrank by another 1,000 wen, to 392,000 wen, with a weak transaction volume of 42,000 strings of wen.

(Silver and Foreign Exchange In and Out) Yesterday's bank settlements for "silver taels": Chinese merchants' settlement notes were 2.78 million, foreign merchants' were 2.45 million, special settlements were 2.89 million, and various cargo, exchange, tax, and miscellaneous settlements were over 13 million. Mortgage transactions were over 1.2 million, and warehouse withdrawals were over 1.3 million. The New York Stock Market is Surging

A report from the Eastern American Bank states that the New York stock market has been strong since Monday. The situation improved further on Tuesday, with strong buying interest from all sides. The market actively trended upward, with significant gains in industrial, railway, and utility stocks. According to official reports, the surge in the stock market on Tuesday was due to President Hoover's speech in Congress, in which he stated that the government would maintain budget equilibrium through sales tax collection and spending reduction policies, which greatly reassured the public. The commodity market was not entirely good. Wheat fell back to 43.75 cents (per bushel), but the cotton market was affected by Wall Street, and closed up to $5.80 per hundred pounds. According to railway industry reports, operating income for the past three months has been excellent, and the total earnings of the business sector in the fourth quarter of this year are expected to be higher than in the same period last year. The Yarn, Flower, and Yarn Markets are Calm

It is Still Difficult for Yarn Factories to Stop Night Work

The cotton yarn market has returned to a calm state, but the situation shows a slight firmness. The proposed reduction in working hours by yarn factories has made people uncertain and most are taking a wait-and-see attitude. As a result, the market has stabilized and customer sales are slightly more active. However, fellow traders purchased 460 bales of 20-count Three Rams yarn because of its cheap price, not because of actual business. Based on the current environment, inventories are too thick, and a large increase is feared to be difficult.

(Auction Yarn in Wait-and-See Mode) The opening price of auction yarn this morning was slightly higher due to the slight increase in American cotton, with each month rising by two or three cents. However, after two or three rounds of bidding, those holding the goods took profits, and the market fell again, with each month falling by three cents. In the afternoon, it was heard that the sales of spot yarn were still good, and people's confidence was slightly boosted. As for the issue of yarn factories stopping night work, it is still difficult to become a reality at present, so the market remains flat, with each month rising by one to four cents. The total transaction volume for the day was 16,400 bales. It was found that Taichang sold 1,100 bales, Xincheng 450 bales, Shenji 350 bales, and Suilong 300 bales. Methods for Ordering Foreign Wheat (Continued) · Zhi · De

(Increase or Decrease in Price) The increase or decrease in the price of foreign or local wheat at the time of exchange delivery is due to differences in quality. Those exceeding the standard wheat are appropriately increased (upgraded), and those below the standard are appropriately reduced (downgraded). The details are described below:

Canadian Wheat: No. 2 wheat with 153 catties is qualified, and the standard is increased by 2 mace and 5 fen. No. 3 wheat with 151 catties is qualified and increased by 2 mace. No. 4 wheat with 149 catties is qualified and increased by 1 mace. Canadian wheat has an average quality. At the time of exchange delivery, it only needs to be based on the original grade to enjoy the standard upgrade.

Australian Wheat: Divided into two types, Western wheat, with a particularly heavy body, can be upgraded by 2 mace and 9 fen according to the standard at the highest. Southern wheat has an average quality, and is upgraded according to the standard by 7 fen to 1 mace. However, the exchange's regulations stipulate that foreign wheat delivered is standardized at 146 catties per Sima scale. The standard is increased by 2 mace and 5 fen, and then increased by 2 fen for each additional catty, increasing sequentially. It will no longer increase beyond 148 catties. 145 catties are increased by 2 mace and 3 fen, 144 catties are increased by 2 mace and 1 fen, 143 catties are increased by 1 mace and 8 fen, 142 catties are increased by 1 mace and 5 fen, 141 catties are increased by 1 mace and 2 fen, 140 catties are increased by 7 fen, and will no longer increase below that.

Chicago Wheat: Its delivery situation is roughly equivalent to Canadian red wheat. Those with 150 catties are increased by 2 mace and 3 fen. Those below 148 catties are unqualified for general orders. Most of them are based on No. 2 wheat.

Domestic Wheat: At the time of exchange delivery, 139 catties to 140 catties per stone (Hai hu) is qualified. Usually, one car (ie, 500 dan) is the unit. Actual delivery can also be changed. The minimum amount is 485 dan, and the maximum amount is 515 dan. If the amount exceeds the specified amount, the excess or shortage shall be calculated at a 95% discount based on the delivery price to indicate the restriction. Usually, the Jinghu car with 30 tons is the standard, because it is suitable for 500 dan. Although the buns in various places are different in size, they are all based on weight. However, the level of delivery is more complicated than foreign wheat.

⑴ Upgrade: 141 catties are increased by 2 fen, 142 catties are increased by 4 fen, and 143 catties are increased by 6 fen at most, and no more will be increased.

⑵ Downgrade: 138 catties are reduced by 2 fen, 137 catties are reduced by 5 fen, 136 catties are reduced by 9 fen, 135 catties are reduced by 1 mace and 3 fen, 134 catties are reduced by 1 mace and 8 fen, 133 catties are reduced by 2 mace and 5 fen, and it will fail and cannot be delivered again. If there are impurities or mud ash in it, 3% is the standard. If there is more or less when sieving, it will be increased or removed accordingly.

Looking at the above grading of this wheat and foreign wheat, there are two kinds of perceptions. First, the highest grade of foreign wheat has reached 2 mace and 9 fen, and the lowest is also about 1 mace. The standard for delivery is 146 catties as qualified at the lowest, and the highest is 148 catties or more. The highest upgrade for this wheat is 6 fen, as if it is already a rare bird. The standard for delivery is 139 catties to 140 catties, and the lowest is 133 catties, which is reduced by 2 mace and 5 fen. Comparing the highest foreign wheat with the lowest standard for this wheat, the difference is as high as 5 mace and 4 fen. The quality of agricultural products is obviously different. Improving planting and improving quality should not be delayed. Moreover, inferior products cannot maintain their original production due to various reasons, so flour mills are only competing to order foreign wheat. It is pitiful and painful. It is urgent to rescue, and the national people have a responsibility for it. (End)

Stable Cotton Market

Manufacturers Occasionally Move in When This Month's Supply is Thrown

The cotton market is still strong, and the situation is stable and quiet. According to the rise in American cotton, spot cotton on the market is scarce. Since a certain factory has thrown out a large batch, it is estimated that there are more than 50,000 in December (ie, the current period). Currently, the source of supply from various sources is very rare and only low prices are occasionally moved in, which makes the market increasingly tight. However, the long-term is not moving but flat. According to a communication from Jinan, there are currently 80,000 to 90,000 bales of cotton in Shandong (wheat price is 41 to 2 yuan per dan). A certain Japanese cotton firm in the area went bankrupt, affecting the market price and causing a sudden drop.

(Each Month's Zheng Standard is Good for Five Cents) The Zheng Standard market opened this morning. Initially, the market rose with the rise in American cotton. After two or three rounds, the market fell again because the yarn market was weak. As a result, it rose by five cents. In the afternoon, the market still had Xincheng shorting, with each month rising by five cents to one mace. The total transaction volume for the day was 24,400 dan. Free Talk

Talking Points

Suicide

— Tian Fang

Suicide, what a cruel term. The increase in suicides is a stark indication of social pathology. Yet, in countries that pride themselves on being "organized," it continues to occur. According to a Tokyo dispatch from the China News Agency on the 2nd,

the Japanese Social Affairs Bureau investigated and found that 1,490 mothers and children committed suicide due to economic panic, unemployment, and starvation. 812 young children were forced to die along with them.

If this telegram were seen by the representatives of the League of Nations in Geneva, I wonder if the Japanese representative Matsuoka, who is currently boasting so loudly, would consider it "regrettable"?

Originally, suicide cases in Japan were well-known. The art of suicide even includes the so-called "seppuku" method, which is said to be necessary to demonstrate "courage." But when a person reaches the point where they do not want to struggle with their environment and resort to suicide, their degree of courage is quite pitiful. This is what is called "Yamato spirit." Due to this cruel way of dealing with oneself, when reflected externally, it creates acts of aggression. This is an inevitable logic.

Historically speaking, Japan during the Sino-Japanese War was certainly different from Japan when it was forced to open trade by American warships. However, the current Japan is also vastly different from Japan during the Russo-Japanese War. After the "Sino-Japanese" and "Sino-Russian" wars, Japan did gain temporary prosperity and embarked on the path of capitalism. However, in recent years, due to the intensification of global economic competition and domestic social recession, the number of unemployed has increased from 480,000 to 500,000 between April of last year and September of this year. (Note: This is a country with a population of 70 million.) The leftward tilt of youth ideology (such as the large-scale strike by 20,000 students at Waseda University last year, and the recent series of major investigations) has particularly caused the authorities headaches. "Ideological guidance" may not be effective with empty words alone. Therefore, by exploring the cracks in the social organization, it can be seen that this "Germany of the East" is facing the danger of "disintegration." Although it is currently maintained by a tense atmosphere, the cracks are deepened by extreme tension. But at this time, the warlords are acting like madmen, recklessly and stubbornly trying to expand. Since forcibly occupying our Eastern Provinces since "September 18th" last year, although the people of our country have suffered losses in life and property, "killing three thousand, injuring eight hundred," the results for Japan have not been favorable. However, exchanging thousands of miles of land for the creation of thousands of orphans and widows has endless future troubles. If our country's economic severance and the armed resistance of the volunteer army can be sustained (not hoping for changes caused by international "competition for the deer"), we can see the collapse of this country, "whose ambitions were not fulfilled before its own destruction," within two years. Therefore, their way of finding a way out is "drowning in the river," more than just "going uphill." And our non-resistance is equivalent to suicide.

Literature and Art

Poem Celebrating the 60th Anniversary of the Shenbao Newspaper

Titled by Xiaoxiang Fisherman

May the trustworthiness and righteousness of the historians of old be celebrated,

May the filial piety and fraternal love that Shen emphasizes uphold ethical principles,

May your newspaper not need the flying geese to deliver its messages,

May your esteemed establishment radiate a phoenix-like aura,

May you emulate Han Fei's six cautions in words and deeds,

May you follow Wei Zheng's ten thoughts to advise against extravagance,

Who still cherishes the order of the Shao martial times?

Let us hope that this newspaper will dispel misfortune from our homeland.

×　×　×　×

May Zhu Zhishan [a calligrapher in Ming] gather the legacy of Sima Qian [a historian in Han],

May Shenbo's [a dignitary in Zhou Dynasty] deeds be made known,

May the best book report follow the tradition of biographies of virtuous officials,

May this building [the newspaper office] echo with the poems of talented scholars,

May the six strategies of Jiang Shang [a military strategist in Zhou] achieve fame and success,

May Su Qin [a strategist in Warring States] not remain unrecognized after ten attempts,

May the discipline emulate the awe and caution of our ancestors,

May these thoughts be held within our hearts.

Science

Organic Pigments

— Reconstruction

There aren't many natural organic pigments, such as indigo, gamboge, and sepia. In addition, there are also things called natural products, but are actually man-made. Organic pigments can be divided into two categories: those extracted from animals or plants, called natural pigments, and those obtained from coal tar, called artificial pigments. Within the scope of dyes, all organic pigments that combine with metal salts to form colored precipitates that are not easily soluble in water are generally called lakes. Several important natural pigments are listed below:

Gamboge丨Gamboge is a natural resin. Its bark is cut away, and a bamboo tube is used to collect the sap that flows out naturally. The juice is steamed off to obtain a yellow gelatinous substance. This gelatinous substance is gamboge. Gamboge has no definite molecular formula. It dissolves in water to form a thick emulsion, making it very suitable for watercolor painting. However, it cannot be directly used in oil paint and must be mixed with aluminum oxide and other fillers before use.

Sepia丨The squid's body has a small sac containing a black juice. It is taken out and dried, dissolved in sodium hydroxide solution, and hydrochloric acid is added, which produces a precipitate. It is filtered, dried to obtain a black pigment, which is durable and easily mixed with other pigments, and is mostly used for color painting.

Burnt Umber丨Made by mixing iron oxide with organic matter. Natural products are available, and it can also be made by burning bone fragments, oak wood, etc. It has strong durability, great hiding power, and is easy to mix with other pigments, so its application is quite wide.

Indigo丨Plants containing indigo originally contain a glucoside in their dry leaves. Indigo and glucose (CoHi2O6) are obtained through fermentation or acid decomposition. However, artificial indigo made from coal tar is now becoming increasingly common, and natural products are gradually being replaced.

Indigo is not easily soluble in water, alcohol, and other solvents and is not greatly affected by dilute acids. It can be dissolved by concentrated sulfuric acid. If sodium hydroxide is added to neutralize it after dissolution, a soluble sodium salt is obtained. The powder obtained by evaporation is the commercial soluble indigo, and its main uses are for making blue ink and coloring animal fibers. Its molecular formula is very complex, and the commonly recognized structural formula is:

C6H4 NH∨ NH4

∧CO Ci一C∧CO ∨ C6H4

Carmine Red丨When female cochineal insects are laying eggs, these insects are collected and steamed to dryness. Boiling carmine red with water yields a beautiful red solution. This pigment has acidic properties and combines with metals or metal oxides to form colored precipitate pigments, also known as lakes. Therefore, carmine red is a red pigment formed by the combination of its acid with aluminum or other metals. The red color is extremely bright, and the color of the compound with aluminum is the best, followed by tin compounds. It is very suitable for painting, coloring, and oil paint applications. It is fairly stable against sunlight, with only slight effects. The chemical molecular formula of carmine red is CiiHi2Oo

Madder Root Red丨Madder root red is mostly produced from the roots of the madder plant. Recently, it is also mostly made from coal tar. It is easily soluble in water and turns reddish-purple when it comes into contact with iodine spirit or caustic soda solution. This liquid combines with various metal oxides to form color lakes of different colors, for example, it becomes red with aluminum oxide, brown with iron oxide, brown with oxide, and red with calcium oxide.

Pigments made from madder root red lack hiding power. The use of this pigment lies in dyeing fibers. When used, it does not directly combine with the fiber; the fiber must first be immersed in a solution of metal salt, and then transferred to a solution of madder root red and boiled to combine. At this time, different metal salts can give different colors fixed on the fiber. Pay attention to this. Also, the main component of madder root red is alizarin, and its formula is as follows:

C6H4 ∧CO

CO∨ C6H2(OH)2

Page 16

Novel

Contradiction

— Bin Fu

The evening breeze made people feel strangely cold. Countless rickshaw pullers huddled and shivered in the corners of the doorways, while Young Master Zhou paced back and forth in the reception room.

Suddenly, the doorbell rang outside, and Young Master Zhou hurried to answer it. A woman dressed in a semi-Western style walked in.

"Let's go, I'm too late." She said this as soon as she entered the door without sitting down.

The man didn't say anything, just looked at the woman's disheveled hair and the bright smile emerging from her crimson lips.

The two walked out.

The position where she carried her satchel on her left arm was now occupied by a man's right arm, and her satchel rested under the man's left arm. They synchronized their steps, walking very slowly. He felt comforted, and she felt happy; everything was warm and cozy.

"Miss Fang, last night at the Central Hotel, hey, thinking about it this morning still makes me feel happy."

"Don't mention it, I've already been scolded by my mother today!"

"Really? Then I'm truly sorry."

"Tch..............."

"My love, look at the falling yellow leaves, what a poetic autumn! Let's not waste such scenery. We're getting tired of watching movies every day; let's take a walk in the park."

The woman pondered for a moment and said:

"I'm sorry, I have a bit of a headache. Let's wait until tomorrow."

"Okay." The man felt a sense of disappointment, but there was no way to object to her.

They arrived at the entrance of a yellow-walled Western-style house.

"Goodbye, I'm sorry, come see me tomorrow." She took back her satchel and released his left hand.

"Hmm,……………………" He walked away in disappointment.

She entered her home, where another handsome face was waiting for her in the reception room:

"Why so late? You're making people wait impatiently." This man approached her, took the satchel from her, and then took her coat, hanging it on the coat rack.

"Are you impatient? Then why did you wait for me?"

"No, no, where? Where? My..., let's go, it's ten to five."

After changing into a brand-new evening gown, she and the man leaned intimately together on their way to the × Grand Theater. He felt comforted, and she felt happy.

×　×　×　×　×

"Yunmei, look at how clear and beautiful the moonlight is!"

"Yes, it's truly beautiful! It's a pity it's a bit cold."

"Are you cold?" He held her even tighter.

"No, I mean the moonlight in the autumn night makes people feel even more desolate. But I think the autumn night is truly full of poetry."

"That's right, I just don't believe people say spring is the most beautiful."

"…………………"

"Yunmei, I truly love you. You're truly my little angel. You're as full of poetry as the autumn night. Only this moonlight can compare to your pure beauty."

He hugged her even closer.

"Yunmei, I think it's getting late; let's go to the Oriental Hotel for a long chat tonight."

"Hmm, okay, tomorrow's homework is those annoying geometry and biology, I'm planning to take a day off."

They decided on their route and began to walk faster. He was infinitely gentle, and she was extremely proud. He felt more comforted, and she felt happier.

Passing by the brightly lit entrance of the Entertainment Square, the glaring lights illuminated the shadowy figures on the sidewalk, all of whom were women. These women's lips were as red as Yunmei's, and these women's hair was as disheveled as Yunmei's. But none of them seemed to be as "poetic" and beautiful as Yunmei, because they were all pursuing men, and no man was cherishing them.

"Ah, look, how pitiful!" She said sentimentally, pointing to the long line of women.

"Yes, selling their bodies isn't enough, they also have to endure the cold and hunger standing here all night! Alas!"

"……………………"

"Let's walk faster, Yunmei…………"

So they headed towards the Oriental Hotel.

Bad Phenomena in Stores Do you want to preserve the store owner's face? Be more assertive and upright

Thoughts on Reading "Colloquial Chinese Language Class"

— Yi Ping

Three years after leaving school, the innocence of that time has been replaced by a mask. When I see many articles in this publication that describe life at school, I dreamily imagine the past; but I don't have the courage to pick up a pen and write about life back then. Today, after reading Master Fo’s "Colloquial Chinese Language Class”, I was reminded of my teacher, Mr. Sun Jingsheng.

Indeed, every student above the junior high school level is unwilling to put in more effort in Chinese language. The reason is that the school authorities pay attention to English, mathematics, and various sciences; it is enough to barely pass Chinese language, and most of the students are there for credits and diplomas. (Of course, I myself was like that too) But three years after leaving school, I have been completely eating by the pen, and I regret my past neglect of Chinese language. Moreover, I cannot help but think of Mr. Sun Jingsheng.

Sun Jingsheng is already over sixty years old and has a beautiful beard, like Mr. Yu Youren, but he is still old and strong, and always tries his best to teach us in class. Unlike other Chinese language teachers who pound the podium and slap the table because students do not listen to his lectures, Mr. Sun always persuades us with gentle words, sometimes even inserting humorous remarks so that we do not feel tired of Chinese language. If the students really fall asleep or prepare for the next lesson, Mr. Sun will definitely declare in advance before a particularly important passage that this passage is very important, implying that students who do not pay attention will have this passage as an exam question in the future. Therefore, the students think of the relationship between credits and devote themselves to this handout again, but there are also times when he deliberately declares this.

There is also the vernacular, which elderly Chinese language teachers always try their best to oppose. They think that what is the point of changing "blue sky" to "blue of the sky". But Mr. Sun is happy to go along with the students, and he is still studying the vernacular himself. Moreover, he welcomes students to his bedroom to chat, anything is fine, even talking about love is fine. There are many things about Mr. Sun. Because I was reminded of the fact that I did not study hard under the patient Mr. Sun when reading "Chinese Language Class", and now I feel the difficulty that the pen is not responding to my heart when I am making a living by the pen, I have written down some miscellaneous feelings.

Shop Assistant Communication

A Difficult Problem

As a staff member, I also manage the accounts. I dare to say that I am diligent in managing affairs and do not dare to neglect my service. However, recently, the store owner's wife (the store owner has other business to attend to, so he does not live here) borrowed 100 dollars from my account due to her smoking and gambling habits, and she has not returned it for a long time. Suddenly, the store owner checked the accounts, and I told him the truth. However, when the store owner asked the store owner's wife, the store owner's wife said, "I entrusted my nephew to give it to him this morning." Later, the store owner came back to my place, and I definitely told him, "I haven't received it." The next day, I met his nephew, and his nephew said to me: "Do you know what happened yesterday? The store owner gave the store owner's wife a big scolding, so the store owner's wife resents you very much, saying that you failed to cover for her. She took advantage of the store owner's absence and gave me the 100 dollars, ordering me to return it to you this morning, and instructing me to tell you to admit your mistake and say that you were unable to find it at the time. But I think such a statement is not appropriate for you, so when the store owner came to the store owner's wife's place for the second time to inquire, I took the responsibility myself and stated: "The store owner's wife did give me this dollar this morning, but I was delayed by other things, so I couldn't send it to the accounting office immediately. It is still in my pocket." This matter was then settled." After listening to it, I deeply admired his wisdom and appreciated his virtue, and I was about to express my gratitude and leave. However, when I thought about the store owner's wife's actions, I didn't know what her intentions were? I am afraid that the outcome will be more ominous than auspicious. How should I deal with this difficult problem in the future? I hope you will not hesitate to share your valuable opinions and give me your advice. I would be very grateful.

Sincerely, Li Ren

December 3rd
